posted:Posted May 21, 2024
msg:Hongtang is really great, highly recommended.

Facilities: The hotel has a sense of design, and the consumables used are all high-end. The hotel's attentiveness and high-end taste can be felt in every detail. It is also the first time I have seen a hotel restaurant use Stokke's children's dining chair (parents with children should know that this dining chair is expensive)

Service: Impeccable, the hotel's service staff are all young people, probably some born in the 2000s, with rare patience and meticulousness. When you get off the boat, someone will greet you at the pier, serve homemade drinks, and accompany you along the way to introduce Hongtang and Gulangyu. Check-in was quick, and the staff for breakfast/afternoon tea/dinner were all very considerate. There was also sweet soup in the evening. It was pouring rain on the day we checked out. The service staff who sent us out arranged a master to send luggage, and also specially took a few transparent umbrellas, saying that they were afraid that we would get wet without umbrellas after getting off the boat. Meticulous service is always the most touching.

Environment: The location is closer to Neicuoao Pier. It is recommended to pay attention when buying boat tickets to avoid walking a lot. The hotel is also good to walk on the hillside, very close to Sunlight Rock and the beach.

Catering: Breakfast is simple but the dishes are very good. The quality of afternoon tea is higher than most five-star hotels. You must try it. Every dish in the Red Pig Restaurant is amazing. The fish skin dumplings are delicious.

I have been to Gulangyu three times and have been to all the places I should go, but because of Hongtang, I will be willing to come again.

BTW, no service staff asked us to write a review, which is really rare, so I am more willing to recommend this hotel.

The best thing is that when I came back and looked through the old photos, I found that I lived in a homestay in the same location of Hongtang 9 years ago. It was really fate.

msg:For the first time in life,
A hotel that I would never leave.

The waiter who picked me up from the ferry terminal was wearing black Chinese overalls, carrying a white canvas bag, and holding a yellow umbrella...

When we arrived at the hotel gate, the girl in white with a big smile came out to greet us...

When we entered the lobby, we were immediately served with welcome tea (Picture 1). We opened our towels, wiped our hands, and drank tea while waiting to check in...

Brother Huang Umbrella and a manager sent us to the room, and explained the facilities and supporting facilities in detail, and even demonstrated how to secure the room door...

Then go to the coffee shop and enjoy the exquisite afternoon tea provided by the hotel. The tables and chairs in the cafe are all medieval, which appeals to my aesthetic taste... What I didn't expect is that the desserts taste better than those in professional shops outside!

Also, after learning that we were here for our wedding anniversary, the hotel immediately upgraded our room for free.

What a surprise.

The hotel is where the famous piano master Yin Chengzong received piano enlightenment from an early age. There are only 13 rooms, and the overall decoration style is retro and high-end. I held my camera and couldn't stop taking pictures...

Breakfast was also very good. Every waiter is kind and polite.

If you come to Gulangyu Island, I highly recommend staying at Hongtang.

msg:The overall design of the hotel is OK. I booked the largest room on the first floor, and the room equipment is quite complete.
But the location is really hard to find, and there's nothing we can do about it. Just ask the butler to show you the way. The service attitude is very good.
But I think there are a few things that are not very good:
One is that the drainage of the toilet is not good and it will be clogged. The water needs to be stopped for a few minutes before flushing to prevent it from overflowing.
Secondly, I know that many people come to Hongtang for the design, but in fact it is really not that amazing. It is still a bit unacceptable to say that this room is carefully designed by the designer, especially at night, the lighting feels quite scary ( See picture)
The third is the free laundry service, which washed my T-shirt from size XL to size M...
The fourth is that the free luggage delivery service is a bit too rude. The mouth of the school bag I received was almost open... (Maybe it was because the uncle ran over too hard...)
The last one is that the coffee shop does not have many self-service items, and the breakfast noodles are basically gone in one bite.
To be honest, a room worth 2,000 yuan could be better.

Facilities: The hotel is located on Gulangyu Island. It was originally built for Christians to gather on weekends. It is constructed of red bricks and wood, and the frame is very beautiful! The current hotel was remodeled in 2009. I asked the housekeeper about the history of the house, and learned that the owner followed the idea of repairing the old as it was, with overall reinforcement + reviewing the history (the old owner‚Äôs father seems to be a relatively simple way of practicing Christianity, Life is about simplicity) Therefore, please cooperate with the designers in Xiamen to build the overall concise, clean, retro and peaceful environment of the Red Hall. I personally like the design of the room very much. There are antique renovations and custom-made furniture. It is equipped with a le labo bath set and a dyson hair dryer. It has retro beauty and the convenience of life provided by modern technology hhh
[Favorite place] The small foyer on the second floor: a window facing the yard, an old table, and a few picture albums. The content is very interesting and the location is very comfortable. One day when I was waiting for breakfast, I read books there for a while, especially Quiet and comfortable, gaining short-term inner peace and happiness.
[About sound insulation] Before booking the money, I saw a friend talking about the sound insulation of the house. My personal experience is as follows. Because it is not a special holiday, there are almost no children. We did not feel too active in the overall guest room. Everyone was very quiet and did not disturb each other. The adjacent alleyway is Fair Road. Originally there were not many tourists. One night, some tourists passed by late. It was a bit noisy, but they left in about 5 minutes, and there was no too much noise after that. If you are really sensitive to sound, you can actually communicate with the store or housekeeper to see if you can book a room facing the courtyard on the 2nd and 3rd floors.

Hygiene: clean and beautiful! The cotton cloth of the bed sheets is very soft and delicate, the room is also bright and clean, and the bathroom is well planned! The supporting yard, red pig restaurant and breakfast tea room are also very comfortable!

Environment: I like it very much. Personally, I prefer quiet places, especially places for rest. The overall a**osphere here is very quiet. Compared with the more lively neighborhood of Sanqiutian, Neicuo'ao is an area where old residents live. If you want to think or sleep well during leisure, I really recommend this place! p.s. I really like the [Second-floor Porch] mentioned above and I also like the [Garden Bench].

Service: I must praise [the butler]! I didn't find out until the review that I didn't remember the name of the housekeeper, sorry! The last time I came to Xiagu as a child, my memory was a lot messy, and I asked the housekeeper many questions about money, and he answered them clearly for us one by one. When boarding the boat, they also communicated with us by phone in advance to determine the exit direction. On the way to the hotel, the history and cultural background of the island and the hotel are also carefully introduced, so that guests can quickly understand the local situation. The housekeepers and staff I met after staying in the hotel were very kind, willing to provide answers, and very patient. Full marks for service!
We have been traveling for a long time and have a lot of luggage. The store kindly invited a porter to help carry the luggage, which greatly relieved the fatigue of carrying luggage. I am very grateful üëçüèª.

[About breakfast] You can choose noodles or rice. If I have a bad stomach, I choose noodles, which are very warm. There are also small side dishes, fried spring rolls or dumplings. The buffet has bread, yogurt, coffee, tea, and fruit. There is a piece of bread with chia seeds that is delicious, especially grassüòÇ. The breakfast room is a wood + glass house that was built later. You can see the mountains and the blue sky and white clouds not far away. Coupled with the beautiful scenery of the yard, the mood is very open.
[About afternoon tea] The check-in gift includes an afternoon tea meal. We arrived late on the first day, so the housekeeper specially extended it to the second day for us, thank you! The taste is very good~sponge cake with salted butter, toasted hazelnut kernels are delicious, and coconut pudding, QQ bouncy~
[Red Pig Restaurant] The hotel's own restaurant, please ask the butler to help you reserve a seat. The restaurant is small and has the feel of a family-style restaurant. I ordered [Red Pork Braised Pork Rice, Abalone Bak Kut Teh, Salt Baked Luncheon Fish, Garlic Shark Lips, and Boiled Choy Heart] and they were all delicious! Not to praise one by one, in short, my family and I are full, and we just go out at night and take a long walk.
The only thing I encountered was a little trouble when I was eating. I met a family with a large number of people eating, so the small restaurant was not very convenient to move around, and it was a little noisy. Fortunately, the food was hot and delicious, so I was not very unhappy. .

[Final addition] Hongtang has its own official account, you can check it in, there are surprises! Visiting the characteristic route is also very informative! Thanks to Hongtang, the housekeeper and all the staff, I like this stay very much, furniture, home decoration, tableware, food, house and people I met, hope to see you again!

msg:The correct way to open Gulangyu Island, the retro texture is beautiful and the red hall~
Many people visit Gulangyu, and they are always in a hurry, so it is easy to overlook and miss a lot of the real beauty and taste of Gulangyu. Therefore, the most comfortable way to play on Gulangyu is to find a quality hotel and stay for a day or two.
.
What I want to share and recommend with you is the HUMBLE HALL Hongtang, a Chinese-style and elegant hotel located on Fair Road, Gulangyu Island. It is a corner of Jing'an and enjoys the unique view of the ancient tree courtyard and the red-roofed villa.
.
The whole space is designed by well-known designers. The lobby, courtyard, coffee shop, guest room, etc., each of which brings people a sense of design and beauty. The high-quality home furnishing with ingenuity and the artistic space a**osphere, come here , more like walking into an art museum full of history on Gulangyu Island.
.
Hongtang currently has 12 guest rooms, each of which is boutique. Top brand home appliances, original antique furniture ornaments, create an extremely luxurious accommodation space.
.
It is fully furnished. The small restaurant on the first floor, Red Pig, and the courtyard cafe STONE BOX under the ancient banyan tree are built on the mountain and have an excellent view. It faces the garden island landscape of Gulangyu Island and the sea view of Xiamen not far away.
.
Coming to Gulangyu and living in such a beautiful and retro quality accommodation is the correct way to open the Gulangyu game~
.

posted:Posted August 5, 2021
msg:Gulangyu Island was scorching hot in summer, away from the noisy tourist routes, and found this quaint building at a cool corner to enjoy the cool, so we immediately decided to live on the island.
The original site is a church that was built in 1936. The entire building rests on a huge rock. Therefore, the stone engraved nameplate of the building is engraved with the words "I will build on this rock". The overall hotel is based on the wood style, with a touch of woody smell in it. The color and taste make people feel that they have passed through the 1930s in an instant, which is very experience. The courtyard behind the hotel is enveloped by banyan trees. When sitting in a daze, you can see the different scenery of Gulangyu Island.
The various small details of the hotel make people feel full of experience. The copper keys and mechanical locks, and various small ornaments can appreciate the intentions of the operators and fit the original identity of the hotel. Under the seemingly simple appearance of the room, the bedding and disposable products are of high quality. The hair dryer is a full set of Dyson. I like the sandalwood fragrance of the toiletries very much. I bought the same style when I came back.
The hotel provides a hearty afternoon tea with a wealth of desserts and drinks. The breakfast is divided into Chinese and Western styles. You can choose by yourself. It is also very hearty. I have the best bowl of seafood noodles I have eaten in Xiamen.
I met the proprietress at afternoon tea, and we had a very happy conversation. During the conversation, I also understood the concept of this hotel, such as the inscription on the key-"The relative stillness of an island". In fact, in addition to exploring new things, the trip itself hopes to keep good memories. Life is hurried, and stopping has become a luxury, but there is always a place where you can stop. It was like that day at the corner of the hotel entrance, we who were forced to stop by the heat, looked up and found the beauty and tranquility here.
